width:25.696ex; height:6.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle v_{\\text{rms}}={\\sqrt {\\frac {3}{2}}}v_{p}={\\sqrt {{3}\\cdot {\\frac {k_{B}T}{m}}}},}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtext>rms</mtext>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msqrt>\n<mfrac>\n<mn>3</mn>\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mfrac>\n</msqrt>\n</mrow>\n<msub>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>p</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msqrt>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>3</mn>\n</mrow>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mrow>\n<msub>\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>B</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mi>T</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mi>m</mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</msqrt>\n</mrow>\n<mo>,</mo>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle v_{\\text{rms}}={\\sqrt {\\frac {3}{2}}}v_{p}={\\sqrt {{3}\\cdot {\\frac {k_{B}T}{m}}}},}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle v_{\\text{rms}}={\\sqrt {\\frac {3}{2}}}v_{p}={\\sqrt {{3}\\cdot {\\frac {k_{B}T}{m}}}},}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202e828e745bb202b62cf4afac97ee5efe12872d" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:27.703ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>where <i>v</i> is in m/s, <i>T</i> is in kelvins, and <i>m</i> is the mass of one molecule of gas. The most probable (or mode) speed <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle v_{\\text{p}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtext>p</mtext>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle v_{\\text{p}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="v_{\\text{p}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8c597064a184e56328af49003c920c966e0d160c" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:2.274ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span> is 81.6% of the rms speed <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle v_{\\text{rms}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtext>rms</mtext>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle v_{\\text{rms}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle v_{\\text{rms}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/70e1acf4a91ad14dffd7c5f0165c539a1407412a" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:4.021ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>, and the mean (arithmetic mean, or average) speed <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle {\\bar {v}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mover>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">&#175;<!-- &#175; --></mo>\n</mover>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle {\\bar {v}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\bar v" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ba1d09340f8f6c1979330c2f23e514e38f243a3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.227ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> is 92.1% of the rms speed (<a href="/wiki/Isotropy" title="Isotropy">isotropic</a> <a href="/wiki/Maxwell%E2%80%93Boltzmann_distribution#Distribution_of_speeds" title="Maxwell&#8211;Boltzmann distribution">distribution of speeds</a>).\n</p><p>See: \n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Average" title="Average">Average</a>,</li>\n<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Root-mean-square_speed" title="Root-mean-square speed">Root-mean-square speed</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Arithmetic_mean" title="Arithmetic mean">Arithmetic mean</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Mean" title="Mean">Mean</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Mode_(statistics)" title="Mode (statistics)">Mode (statistics)</a></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Transport_properties">Transport properties</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kinetic_theory_of_gases&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Transport properties">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/Transport_phenomena" title="Transport phenomena">Transport phenomena</a></div>\n<p>The kinetic theory of gases deals not only with gases in thermodynamic equilibrium, but also very importantly with gases not in thermodynamic equilibrium. This means using Kinetic Theory to consider what are known as "transport properties", such as <a href="/wiki/Mass_diffusivity" title="Mass diffusivity">mass diffusivity</a>, <a href="/wiki/Viscosity" title="Viscosity">viscosity</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thermal_conductivity" title="Thermal conductivity">thermal conductivity</a>. The following discussion are all based on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Transport_equation" title="Transport equation">transport equation</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Diffusion_Coefficient_and_diffusion_flux">Diffusion Coefficient and diffusion flux</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kinetic_theory_of_gases&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Diffusion Coefficient and diffusion flux">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/Fick%27s_laws_of_diffusion" title="Fick\'s laws of diffusion">Fick\'s laws of diffusion</a></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Viscosity_and_kinetic_momentum">Viscosity and kinetic momentum</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kinetic_theory_of_gases&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Viscosity and kinetic momentum">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/Viscosity#Momentum_transport" title="Viscosity">Viscosity &#167;&#160;Momentum transport</a></div>\n<p>In books on elementary kinetic theory<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sears1975_21-0"><a href="#cite_note-Sears1975-21">[21]</a></sup> one can find results for dilute gas modeling that has widespread use. \nDerivation of the kinetic model for shear viscosity usually starts by considering a <a href="/wiki/Couette_flow" title="Couette flow">Couette flow</a> where two parallel plates are separated by a gas layer. The upper plate is moving at a constant velocity to the right due to a force F. The lower plate is stationary, and an equal and opposite force must therefore be acting on it to keep it at rest. The molecules in the gas layer have a forward velocity component <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle u}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>u</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle u}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="u" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3e6bb763d22c20916ed4f0bb6bd49d7470cffd8" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> which increase uniformly with distance <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>y</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle y}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="y" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8a6208ec717213d4317e666f1ae872e00620a0d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.155ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> above the lower plate. The non-equilibrium flow is superimposed on a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maxwell-Boltzmann_distribution" title="Maxwell-Boltzmann distribution">Maxwell-Boltzmann equilibrium distribution</a> of molecular motions.\n</p><p>Let <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\sigma }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\sigma }</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\sigma " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/59f59b7c3e6fdb1d0365a494b81fb9a696138c36" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> be the collision <a href="/wiki/Cross_section_(physics)#Collision_among_gas_particles" title="Cross section (physics)">cross section</a> of one molecule colliding with another. The number density <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>C</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle C}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="C" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4fc55753007cd3c18576f7933f6f089196732029" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.766ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> is defined as the number of molecules per (extensive) volume <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle C=N/V}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>C</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mo>/</mo>\n</mrow>\n<mi>V</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle C=N/V}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle C=N/V}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1af7d3eafd42c4ea8a0d2563de5fb0fb0582de4b" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:9.878ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>. The collision cross section per volume or collision cross section density is <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle C\\sigma }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>C</mi>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle C\\sigma }</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle C\\sigma }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b22bd4789d67f9555a8e964e6a5c1f4df763b40c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.096ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>, and it is related to the <a href="/wiki/Mean_free_path#Mean_free_path_in_kinetic_theory" title="Mean free path">mean free path</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle l}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>l</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle l}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="l" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/829091f745070b9eb97a80244129025440a1cfac" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.693ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> by \n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad l={\\frac {1}{{\\sqrt {2}}C\\sigma }}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<mi>l</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msqrt>\n<mn>2</mn>\n</msqrt>\n</mrow>\n<mi>C</mi>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad l={\\frac {1}{{\\sqrt {2}}C\\sigma }}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad l={\\frac {1}{{\\sqrt {2}}C\\sigma }}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ecdbbb2d52d12e02fa98bb5cd704a3fe2cdfeea2" style="vertical-align: -2.838ex; width:13.145ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>Notice that the unit of the collision cross section per volume <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle C\\sigma }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>C</mi>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle C\\sigma }</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle C\\sigma }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b22bd4789d67f9555a8e964e6a5c1f4df763b40c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.096ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> is reciprocal of length. The mean free path is the average distance traveled by a molecule, or a number of molecules per volume, before they make their first collision.\n</p><p>Let <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle u_{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>u</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle u_{0}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle u_{0}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9c7425f9c7ab645587060423c0af62f8a61fbc65" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.384ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> be the forward velocity of the gas at an imaginary horizontal surface inside the gas layer. On the average, a molecule that crosses the surface makes its last collision before crossing at a distance equal to two-thirds of the mean free path (i.e. <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle 2l/3}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mn>2</mn>\n<mi>l</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mo>/</mo>\n</mrow>\n<mn>3</mn>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle 2l/3}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle 2l/3}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8db2a93ec8dac2c7510561d9020af23959ba974b" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.181ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>) away from the surface. At this distance above and below the surface, the forward momentum of the molecule is respectively\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad p_{x}^{\\pm }=m\\left(u_{0}\\pm {\\frac {2}{3}}l{du \\over dy}\\right)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<msubsup>\n<mi>p</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>x</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mo>&#177;<!-- &#177; --></mo>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi>m</mi>\n<mrow>\n<mo>(</mo>\n<mrow>\n<msub>\n<mi>u</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>&#177;<!-- &#177; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>2</mn>\n<mn>3</mn>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mi>l</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mrow>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>u</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>y</mi>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n<mo>)</mo>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad p_{x}^{\\pm }=m\\left(u_{0}\\pm {\\frac {2}{3}}l{du \\over dy}\\right)}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad p_{x}^{\\pm }=m\\left(u_{0}\\pm {\\frac {2}{3}}l{du \\over dy}\\right)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ce0c6e2a72a23b6169d77e4a67b37dc01b57c649" style="vertical-align: -2.505ex; width:25.248ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>where m is the molecular mass. The molecular flux  <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\Phi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi mathvariant="normal">&#934;<!-- &#934; --></mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\Phi }</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\Phi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/aed80a2011a3912b028ba32a52dfa57165455f24" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> includes all molecules arriving at one side of an element of the surface within the gas layer. The incoming molecules are coming from all directions at the one side of the surface and with all speeds. This molecular flux (i.e. the number flux) is related to the average molecular speed <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle {\\bar {v}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mover>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">&#175;<!-- &#175; --></mo>\n</mover>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle {\\bar {v}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle {\\bar {v}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ba1d09340f8f6c1979330c2f23e514e38f243a3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.227ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> by\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\Phi ={\\frac {1}{4}}{\\bar {v}}C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<mi mathvariant="normal">&#934;<!-- &#934; --></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mn>4</mn>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mover>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">&#175;<!-- &#175; --></mo>\n</mover>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n<mi>C</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad \\Phi ={\\frac {1}{4}}{\\bar {v}}C}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\Phi ={\\frac {1}{4}}{\\bar {v}}C}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a2cc67af4322a5e3b0f2c06f3858f36f601c6734" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:12.091ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>Notice that the forward velocity gradient <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle du/dy}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>u</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mo>/</mo>\n</mrow>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>y</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle du/dy}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle du/dy}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/128cb53bd4b702d840ae52abfe488684a8aa3d31" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.079ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> can be considered to be constant over a distance of mean free path. Next we multiply by the total flux to get the change of momentum per unit time and per unit area, that is carried by the molecules crossing from either above or below the surface area. This gives the equation\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\Phi p_{x}^{\\pm }={\\frac {1}{4}}{\\bar {v}}C\\cdot m\\left(u_{0}\\pm {\\frac {2}{3}}l{du \\over dy}\\right)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<mi mathvariant="normal">&#934;<!-- &#934; --></mi>\n<msubsup>\n<mi>p</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>x</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mo>&#177;<!-- &#177; --></mo>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mn>4</mn>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mover>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">&#175;<!-- &#175; --></mo>\n</mover>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n<mi>C</mi>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<mi>m</mi>\n<mrow>\n<mo>(</mo>\n<mrow>\n<msub>\n<mi>u</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>&#177;<!-- &#177; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>2</mn>\n<mn>3</mn>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mi>l</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mrow>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>u</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>y</mi>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n<mo>)</mo>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad \\Phi p_{x}^{\\pm }={\\frac {1}{4}}{\\bar {v}}C\\cdot m\\left(u_{0}\\pm {\\frac {2}{3}}l{du \\over dy}\\right)}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\Phi p_{x}^{\\pm }={\\frac {1}{4}}{\\bar {v}}C\\cdot m\\left(u_{0}\\pm {\\frac {2}{3}}l{du \\over dy}\\right)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9b4d1c13a6e492da1995874d82c19eeb48a1552c" style="vertical-align: -2.505ex; width:33.597ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>The net rate of momentum per unit area that is transported across the imaginary surface is thus\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\tau =\\Phi p_{x}^{+}-\\Phi p_{x}^{-}={\\frac {1}{3}}{\\bar {v}}Cm\\cdot l{du \\over dy}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<mi>&#964;<!-- &#964; --></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi mathvariant="normal">&#934;<!-- &#934; --></mi>\n<msubsup>\n<mi>p</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>x</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mo>+</mo>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mi mathvariant="normal">&#934;<!-- &#934; --></mi>\n<msubsup>\n<mi>p</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>x</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mn>3</mn>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mover>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">&#175;<!-- &#175; --></mo>\n</mover>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n<mi>C</mi>\n<mi>m</mi>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<mi>l</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mrow>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>u</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>y</mi>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad \\tau =\\Phi p_{x}^{+}-\\Phi p_{x}^{-}={\\frac {1}{3}}{\\bar {v}}Cm\\cdot l{du \\over dy}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\tau =\\Phi p_{x}^{+}-\\Phi p_{x}^{-}={\\frac {1}{3}}{\\bar {v}}Cm\\cdot l{du \\over dy}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ca828c15c73669e55661e6e3a2448e698df352fe" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:34.065ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>The defining equation for the (shear) viscosity <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\eta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>&#951;<!-- &#951; --></mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\eta }</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\eta " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e4d701857cf5fbec133eebaf94deadf722537f64" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:1.169ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> of the gas is\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad {\\frac {F}{A}}=\\eta {du \\over dy}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mi>F</mi>\n<mi>A</mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi>&#951;<!-- &#951; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mrow>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>u</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mi>y</mi>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad {\\frac {F}{A}}=\\eta {du \\over dy}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad {\\frac {F}{A}}=\\eta {du \\over dy}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c9e24babd0fd696fc273b15d26fd1085c95251bc" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:12.551ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>Combining the above kinetic equation with defining equation for (shear) viscosity by <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\tau =F/A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>&#964;<!-- &#964; --></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi>F</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mo>/</mo>\n</mrow>\n<mi>A</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\tau =F/A}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\tau =F/A}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/22f373a47fc8548cf14fe51a206b2056c520c0a6" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.947ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> gives the equation for shear viscosity, which is usually denoted <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\eta _{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>&#951;<!-- &#951; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\eta _{0}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt=" \\eta_{0} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ef3886c3f161b7f02d23221bfead21a18ffb82ff" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:2.21ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> when it is a dilute gas:\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\eta _{0}={\\frac {1}{3}}{\\bar {v}}Cml}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<msub>\n<mi>&#951;<!-- &#951; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mn>3</mn>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mover>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">&#175;<!-- &#175; --></mo>\n</mover>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n<mi>C</mi>\n<mi>m</mi>\n<mi>l</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad \\eta _{0}={\\frac {1}{3}}{\\bar {v}}Cml}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\eta _{0}={\\frac {1}{3}}{\\bar {v}}Cml}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/612e21ccdfa5311b03b019805f7779653eec1a83" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:15.356ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>Combining this equation with the equation for mean free path gives\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\eta _{0}={\\frac {1}{3{\\sqrt {2}}}}{\\frac {m\\cdot {\\bar {v}}}{\\sigma }}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<msub>\n<mi>&#951;<!-- &#951; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mrow>\n<mn>3</mn>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msqrt>\n<mn>2</mn>\n</msqrt>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mrow>\n<mi>m</mi>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mover>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">&#175;<!-- &#175; --></mo>\n</mover>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad \\eta _{0}={\\frac {1}{3{\\sqrt {2}}}}{\\frac {m\\cdot {\\bar {v}}}{\\sigma }}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\eta _{0}={\\frac {1}{3{\\sqrt {2}}}}{\\frac {m\\cdot {\\bar {v}}}{\\sigma }}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/92e1f3f93a3019f0a7dcd62027f17933239d0245" style="vertical-align: -2.838ex; width:18.51ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>From statistical thermodynamics for gases we have equations relating average molecular speed to most likely speed and further to temperature. These statistical results gives the average (equilibrium) molecular speed as\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad {\\bar {v}}={\\frac {2}{\\sqrt {\\pi }}}v_{p}=2{\\sqrt {{\\frac {2}{\\pi }}\\cdot {\\frac {k_{B}T}{m_{}}}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mover>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">&#175;<!-- &#175; --></mo>\n</mover>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>2</mn>\n<msqrt>\n<mi>&#960;<!-- &#960; --></mi>\n</msqrt>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<msub>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>p</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>2</mn>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msqrt>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>2</mn>\n<mi>&#960;<!-- &#960; --></mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mrow>\n<msub>\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>B</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mi>T</mi>\n</mrow>\n<msub>\n<mi>m</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</msqrt>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad {\\bar {v}}={\\frac {2}{\\sqrt {\\pi }}}v_{p}=2{\\sqrt {{\\frac {2}{\\pi }}\\cdot {\\frac {k_{B}T}{m_{}}}}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad {\\bar {v}}={\\frac {2}{\\sqrt {\\pi }}}v_{p}=2{\\sqrt {{\\frac {2}{\\pi }}\\cdot {\\frac {k_{B}T}{m_{}}}}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0c663f5ffdb17714268ea83515845fbb9568b9af" style="vertical-align: -2.838ex; width:28.534ex; height:6.676ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>where <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle v_{p}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>v</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>p</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle v_{p}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle v_{p}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/537e72b1a70774ae976de89f7919dc0e0a9bb86d" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:2.187ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span> is the most probable speed, <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle k_{B}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>B</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle k_{B}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle k_{B}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/70f38f7b73e53fd7b5d9ca64bec3a1438cc0eade" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.691ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> is the Boltzmann constant. We note that\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad k_{B}\\cdot N_{A}=R\\quad {\\text{and}}\\quad M=m\\cdot N_{A}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<msub>\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>B</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>A</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi>R</mi>\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtext>and</mtext>\n</mrow>\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<mi>M</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi>m</mi>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>A</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad k_{B}\\cdot N_{A}=R\\quad {\\text{and}}\\quad M=m\\cdot N_{A}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad k_{B}\\cdot N_{A}=R\\quad {\\text{and}}\\quad M=m\\cdot N_{A}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7b4bf725bb06cb15f921245261a7ac18c5805e73" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:35.87ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>and insert the velocity in the viscosity equation above. This gives the well known equation for shear viscosity for dilute gases:\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\eta _{0}={\\frac {2}{3{\\sqrt {\\pi }}}}\\cdot {\\frac {\\sqrt {mk_{B}T}}{\\sigma }}={\\frac {2}{3{\\sqrt {\\pi }}}}\\cdot {\\frac {\\sqrt {MRT}}{\\sigma \\cdot N_{A}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<msub>\n<mi>&#951;<!-- &#951; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>2</mn>\n<mrow>\n<mn>3</mn>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msqrt>\n<mi>&#960;<!-- &#960; --></mi>\n</msqrt>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<msqrt>\n<mi>m</mi>\n<msub>\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>B</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mi>T</mi>\n</msqrt>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>2</mn>\n<mrow>\n<mn>3</mn>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msqrt>\n<mi>&#960;<!-- &#960; --></mi>\n</msqrt>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<msqrt>\n<mi>M</mi>\n<mi>R</mi>\n<mi>T</mi>\n</msqrt>\n<mrow>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mo>&#8901;<!-- &#8901; --></mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>A</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad \\eta _{0}={\\frac {2}{3{\\sqrt {\\pi }}}}\\cdot {\\frac {\\sqrt {mk_{B}T}}{\\sigma }}={\\frac {2}{3{\\sqrt {\\pi }}}}\\cdot {\\frac {\\sqrt {MRT}}{\\sigma \\cdot N_{A}}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\eta _{0}={\\frac {2}{3{\\sqrt {\\pi }}}}\\cdot {\\frac {\\sqrt {mk_{B}T}}{\\sigma }}={\\frac {2}{3{\\sqrt {\\pi }}}}\\cdot {\\frac {\\sqrt {MRT}}{\\sigma \\cdot N_{A}}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6215e1dcbc87368571a730d7249f9148a96e9929" style="vertical-align: -2.838ex; width:42.762ex; height:7.176ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>and <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle M}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>M</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle M}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="M" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f82cade9898ced02fdd08712e5f0c0151758a0dd" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.442ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> is the molar mass. The equation above presupposes that the gas density is low (i.e. the pressure is low). This implies that the kinetic translational energy dominates over rotational and vibrational molecule energies. The viscosity equation further presupposes that there is only one type of gas molecules, and that the gas molecules are perfect elastic and hard core particles of spherical shape. This assumption of elastic, hard core spherical molecules, like billiard balls, implies that the collision cross section of one molecule can be estimated by\n</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\sigma =\\pi \\left(2r\\right)^{2}=\\pi d^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mspace width="1em"></mspace>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi>&#960;<!-- &#960; --></mi>\n<msup>\n<mrow>\n<mo>(</mo>\n<mrow>\n<mn>2</mn>\n<mi>r</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mo>)</mo>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msup>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi>&#960;<!-- &#960; --></mi>\n<msup>\n<mi>d</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msup>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\quad \\sigma =\\pi \\left(2r\\right)^{2}=\\pi d^{2}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle \\quad \\sigma =\\pi \\left(2r\\right)^{2}=\\pi d^{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3cc716ce362fad9c0e3859459599047069327ddc" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:19.86ex; height:3.343ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>The radius <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle r}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>r</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle r}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="r" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0d1ecb613aa2984f0576f70f86650b7c2a132538" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.049ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> is called collision cross section radius or kinetic radius, and the diameter <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle d}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>d</mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle d}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="d" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e85ff03cbe0c7341af6b982e47e9f90d235c66ab" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.216ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> is called collision cross section diameter or <a href="/wiki/Kinetic_diameter" title="Kinetic diameter">kinetic diameter</a> of a molecule in a monomolecular gas. There are no simple general relation between the collision <a href="/wiki/Cross_section_(physics)#Collision_among_particles" title="Cross section (physics)">cross section</a> and the hard core size of the (fairly spherical) molecule. The relation depends on shape of the potential energy of the molecule. For a real spherical molecule (i.e. a noble gas atom or a reasonably spherical molecule) the interaction potential is more like the <a href="/wiki/Lennard-Jones_potential" title="Lennard-Jones potential">Lennard-Jones potential</a> or <a href="/wiki/Morse_potential" title="Morse potential">Morse potential</a> which have a negative part that attracts the other molecule from distances longer than the hard core radius. <a href="/wiki/Mean_free_path#Mean_free_path_in_kinetic_theory" title="Mean free path">The radius for zero  Lennard-Jones potential</a> is then appropriate to use as estimate for the kinetic radius.\n</p><p>Local nomenclature list:\n</p>\n<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: Burnett, Cambridge University Press, London.</li>\n<li>J. O. Hirschfelder, C. F. Curtiss, and R. B. Bird (1964).  <i>Molecular Theory of Gases and Liquids</i>, second edition (Wiley).</li>\n<li>R. L.
